### [64] [RAG over Thinking Traces Can Improve Reasoning Tasks](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03344v2)
*Negar Arabzadeh,Wenjie Ma,Sewon Min,Matei Zaharia*

Main category: cs.IR

Selection reason: RAG over thinking traces提升推理任务，涉及代码生成benchmark，对agent推理增强有启发。

TL;DR: 通过检索思考轨迹而非文档，RAG在推理任务（如数学和代码生成）上显著提升了强模型性能，挑战了RAG对推理任务帮助有限的普遍看法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 挑战RAG对推理密集型任务（如数学、代码生成）帮助有限的普遍假设，揭示限制在于语料选择而非RAG本身。

Method: 提出T3方法，将问题求解过程中的中间思考轨迹转化为结构化、检索友好的表示，并采用简单的检索-生成（Retrieve-then-Generate）管道进行推理增强。

Result: 在AIME 2025-2026、LiveCodeBench和GPQA-Diamond等基准上，使用思考轨迹的RAG持续超越非RAG基线和检索标准网络语料的方法，例如在AIME上对Gemini-2.5-Flash等模型实现+56.3%的相对提升。

Conclusion: 思考轨迹是推理任务的有效检索语料，将其转化为结构化、紧凑或诊断性表示可进一步解锁更强性能增益。

中文摘要：检索增强生成（RAG）在知识密集型任务中已被证明有效，但普遍认为其对数学和代码生成等推理密集型问题的帮助有限。我们通过展示限制不在于RAG本身而在于语料选择来挑战这一假设。我们不检索文档，而是提出检索思考轨迹，即问题求解过程中产生的中间思考路径。我们证明了思考轨迹本身就是一个强大的检索源，并进一步引入了T3，一种离线方法，将其转化为结构化、利于检索的表示，以提高可用性。使用这些轨迹作为语料，一个简单的检索-生成流程在强模型和基准测试（如AIME 2025-2026、LiveCodeBench和GPQA-Diamond）上持续提升推理性能，优于非RAG基线和标准网络语料检索。例如，在AIME 2025-2026上，使用Gemini-2-thinking生成的轨迹进行RAG，对Gemini-2.5-Flash、GPT-OSS-120B和GPT-5分别实现了+56.3%、+8.6%和+7.6%的相对提升，尽管这些是更新的模型。总体而言，我们的结果表明，思考轨迹是推理任务的有效检索语料，将其转化为结构化、紧凑或诊断性表示能解锁更强的增益。代码见https://github.com/Narabzad/t3。

Original abstract: Retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) has proven effective for knowledge-intensive tasks, but is widely believed to offer limited benefit for reasoning-intensive problems such as math and code generation. We challenge this assumption by showing that the limitation lies not in RAG itself, but in the choice of corpus. Instead of retrieving documents, we propose retrieving thinking traces, i.e., intermediate thinking trajectories generated during problem solving attempts. We show that thinking traces are already a strong retrieval source, and further introduce T3, an offline method that transforms them into structured, retrieval-friendly representations, to improve usability. Using these traces as a corpus, a simple retrieve-then-generate pipeline consistently improves reasoning performance across strong models and benchmarks such as AIME 2025--2026, LiveCodeBench, and GPQA-Diamond, outperforming both non-RAG baselines and retrieval over standard web corpora. For instance, on AIME 2025-2026, RAG with traces generated by Gemini-2-thinking achieves relative gains of +56.3%, +8.6%, and +7.6% for Gemini-2.5-Flash, GPT-OSS-120B, and GPT-5, respectively, even though these are more recent models. Overall, our results suggest that thinking traces are an effective retrieval corpus for reasoning tasks, and transforming them into structured, compact, or diagnostic representations unlocks even stronger gains. Code available at https://github.com/Narabzad/t3.

</details>


### [65] [Decision-aware User Simulation Agent for Evaluating Conversational Recommender Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05250v1)
*Yuan-Chi Li,Li-Chi Chen,Sung-Yi Wu,Yu-Che Tsai,Shou-De Lin*

Main category: cs.IR

Selection reason: 决策感知用户模拟agent，可迁移至agent评估

TL;DR: Hesitator是一个基于理论的用户模拟框架，显式建模选择超载下的人类决策，用于对话推荐系统的自动评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有用户模拟器未能模拟真实的人类决策，特别是在选择超载下的犹豫和延迟，导致接受概率过高。

Method: 提出模块化决策模块，将基于效用的物品选择与感知超载的承诺决策分离。

Result: 在多个框架、领域、销售模式和LLM骨干上的实验表明，该模块在超载增加时持续缓解不切实际的行为，并再现心理经济学中的行为模式。

Conclusion: Hesitator有效模拟了对话推荐系统评估中的人类决策行为。

中文摘要：对话推荐系统（CRS）日益依赖用户模拟器对销售代理进行自动评估。此类模拟器的一个关键要求是能够模拟人类决策。然而，现有大多数模拟框架并未显式建模内部决策过程，且基于LLM的模拟器通常表现出不切实际的强大信息处理能力，很少展现真实消费者行为中常见的犹豫或决策延迟，导致接受概率过高。为解决这一局限，我们提出Hesitator，一个基于理论的用户模拟框架，显式建模选择超载下的人类决策。该框架引入模块化决策模块，将基于效用的物品选择与感知超载的承诺决策分离。在多个用户模拟框架、领域、销售模式和LLM骨干上的实验表明，集成我们的模块能在超载条件增加时持续缓解不切实际的行为。此外，Hesitator再现了心理经济学中的既定行为模式，证明了其模拟人类决策行为的能力。

Original abstract: Conversational recommender systems (CRS) increasingly rely on user simulators for automated evaluation of sales agents. A key requirement for such simulators is the ability to model human decision-making. However, most existing simulation frameworks do not explicitly model the internal decision process, and LLM-based simulators often exhibit unrealistically strong information-processing capabilities, rarely exhibit the hesitation or decision deferral commonly observed in real consumer behavior, resulting in overly high acceptance probabilities. To address this limitation, we propose Hesitator, a theory-grounded user simulation framework that explicitly models human decision-making under choice overload. The framework introduces a modular Decision Module that separates utility-based item selection from overload-aware commitment decisions. Experiments across multiple user simulation frameworks, domains, sales modes, and LLM backbones show that integrating our module consistently mitigates unrealistic behaviors under increasing overload conditions. Furthermore, Hesitator reproduces established behavioral patterns from psychological economics, demonstrating its ability to model human decision behavior.

</details>

# cs.DB [[Back]](#toc)

### [66] [FINER-SQL: Boosting Small Language Models for Text-to-SQL](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03465v1)
*Thanh Dat Hoang,Thanh Trung Huynh,Matthias Weidlich,Thanh Tam Nguyen,Tong Chen,Hongzhi Yin,Quoc Viet Hung Nguyen*

Main category: cs.DB

Selection reason: FINER-SQL通过细粒度执行反馈强化学习提升小模型Text-to-SQL生成，奖励设计可迁移至代码优化agent。

TL;DR: FINER-SQL通过细粒度执行反馈的强化学习框架，有效提升了小语言模型在Text-to-SQL任务上的性能，实现了与大型语言模型相当的执行准确率，同时显著降低了推理延迟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型在Text-to-SQL任务中表现优异但存在计算成本高、延迟长和数据隐私问题；小型语言模型则因推理能力弱和指令遵循差而性能不佳；传统的稀疏二进制奖励强化学习方法在SQL错误时缺乏有效学习信号，导致训练不稳定。

Method: 提出FINER-SQL框架，基于群体相对策略优化（GRPO），引入两种细粒度奖励函数：记忆奖励（通过验证轨迹保持语义稳定性）和原子奖励（衡量操作级重叠以对部分正确SQL给予部分分数），将离散正确性转化为连续学习信号，实现稳定无批评家的优化。

Result: 在BIRD和Spider基准上，使用3B模型分别达到67.73%和85%的执行准确率，与大型语言模型性能相当，同时推理延迟仅5.57秒/样本。

Conclusion: FINER-SQL提供了一条成本高效且保护隐私的Text-to-SQL生成路径，通过细粒度反馈使小型语言模型能够匹敌大型模型的性能，适合实际部署。

中文摘要：大型语言模型在Text-to-SQL生成方面取得了重大进展。然而，它们存在计算成本高、延迟长和数据隐私问题，这使得它们在许多实际应用中不实用。一个自然的替代方案是使用小型语言模型（SLM），它能够实现高效且私密的本地部署。然而，SLM通常难以处理弱推理和较差的指令遵循能力。基于稀疏二进制奖励（0/1）的传统强化学习方法在生成的SQL不正确时提供的学习信号很少，导致训练不稳定或崩溃。为了克服这些问题，我们提出了FINER-SQL，这是一个可扩展且可重用的强化学习框架，通过细粒度执行反馈来增强SLM。基于群体相对策略优化，FINER-SQL用密集且可解释的奖励取代了稀疏监督，即使对于不正确的SQL也能提供连续反馈。它引入了两个关键奖励函数：记忆奖励，它将推理与经过验证的轨迹对齐以实现语义稳定性；以及原子奖励，它衡量操作级别的重叠，以便为结构正确但不完整的SQL赋予部分分数。这种方法将离散的正确性转化为连续学习，实现了稳定且无批评家的优化。在BIRD和Spider基准上的实验表明，FINER-SQL在3B模型上分别达到了67.73%和85%的执行准确率——与更大的LLM相当，同时将推理延迟降低到每样本5.57秒。这些结果突显了一条通向高性能Text-to-SQL生成的高性价比且保护隐私的路径。我们的代码可在https://github.com/thanhdath/finer-sql获取。

Original abstract: Large language models have driven major advances in Text-to-SQL generation. However, they suffer from high computational cost, long latency, and data privacy concerns, which make them impractical for many real-world applications. A natural alternative is to use small language models (SLMs), which enable efficient and private on-premise deployment. Yet, SLMs often struggle with weak reasoning and poor instruction following. Conventional reinforcement learning methods based on sparse binary rewards (0/1) provide little learning signal when the generated SQLs are incorrect, leading to unstable or collapsed training. To overcome these issues, we propose FINER-SQL, a scalable and reusable reinforcement learning framework that enhances SLMs through fine-grained execution feedback. Built on group relative policy optimization, FINER-SQL replaces sparse supervision with dense and interpretable rewards that offer continuous feedback even for incorrect SQLs. It introduces two key reward functions: a memory reward, which aligns reasoning with verified traces for semantic stability, and an atomic reward, which measures operation-level overlap to grant partial credit for structurally correct but incomplete SQLs. This approach transforms discrete correctness into continuous learning, enabling stable, critic-free optimization. Experiments on the BIRD and Spider benchmarks show that FINER-SQL achieves up to 67.73\% and 85\% execution accuracy with a 3B model -- matching much larger LLMs while reducing inference latency to 5.57~s/sample. These results highlight a cost-efficient and privacy-preserving path toward high-performance Text-to-SQL generation. Our code is available at https://github.com/thanhdath/finer-sql.

</details>

# cs.CV [[Back]](#toc)

### [67] [Enhancing Self-Supervised Talking Head Forgery Detection via a Training-Free Dual-System Framework](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03390v1)
*Ke Liu,Jiwei Wei,Shuchang Zhou,Yutong Xiao,Ruikun Chai,Yitong Qin,Yuyang Zhou,Yang Yang*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 双系统框架（System-1/System-2）用于伪造检测，可迁移至agent的快速慢速推理设计。

TL;DR: 提出一种无训练的双系统框架（TFDS），通过先粗筛再细粒度推理的方式提升现有自监督说话人伪造检测器的判别能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于分数的自监督检测器在困难样本上排序不可靠，判别能力未充分利用，需进一步优化。

Method: TFDS框架：系统-1使用阈值路由将样本分为置信和不确定子集；系统-2对不确定子集进行细粒度证据引导推理，优化分数分布中的相对排序。

Result: 在多个数据集和扰动设置下均取得一致改进，改进主要源于不确定子集内排序的纠正。

Conclusion: 现有自监督说话人伪造检测器仍存在未充分利用的判别线索，可通过无训练双系统推理有效解锁。

中文摘要：监督式说话人伪造检测由于生成器的持续演化而面临严峻的泛化挑战。通过减少对特定生成器伪造模式的依赖，自监督检测器提供了更强的跨生成器鲁棒性。然而，现有研究主要关注构建更强的检测器，而训练好的检测器的判别能力尚未得到充分利用。特别是对于基于分数的自监督检测器，在困难样本上的判别能力有限通常表现为不可靠的异常排序，这为进一步优化留下了空间。受此观察启发，我们从人类认知的双系统理论中汲取灵感，提出了一个无训练的双系统（TFDS）框架，以进一步挖掘现有基于分数的自监督检测器的潜在判别能力。TFDS将类似异常的分数作为系统-1的基础，使用轻量级基于阈值的路由将样本划分为置信子集和不确定子集。然后系统-2仅重新审视不确定子集，进行细粒度的证据引导推理，以优化原始分数分布中模糊样本的相对排序。大量实验表明，在不同数据集和扰动设置下均取得一致改进，这些改进主要源于不确定子集内排序的纠正。这些发现表明，现有的自监督说话人伪造检测器中仍然存在未被充分利用的判别线索，可以通过无训练的双系统推理有效解锁。

Original abstract: Supervised talking head forgery detection faces severe generalization challenges due to the continuous evolution of generators. By reducing reliance on generator-specific forgery patterns, self-supervised detectors offer stronger cross-generator robustness. However, existing research has mainly focused on building stronger detectors, while the discriminative capacity of trained detectors remains insufficiently exploited. In particular, for score-based self-supervised detectors, the limited discriminative ability on hard cases is often reflected in unreliable anomaly ordering, leaving room for further refinement. Motivated by this observation, we draw inspiration from the dual-system theory of human cognition and propose a Training-Free Dual-System (TFDS) framework to further exploit the latent discriminative capacity of existing score-based self-supervised detectors. TFDS treats anomaly-like scores as the basis of System-1, using lightweight threshold-based routing to partition samples into confident and uncertain subsets. System-2 then revisits only the uncertain subset, performing fine-grained evidence-guided reasoning to refine the relative ordering of ambiguous samples within the original score distribution. Extensive experiments demonstrate consistent improvements across datasets and perturbation settings, with the gains arising mainly from corrected ordering within the uncertain subset. These findings show that existing self-supervised talking head forgery detectors still contain underexploited discriminative cues that can be effectively unlocked through training-free dual-system reasoning.

</details>


### [68] [iWorld-Bench: A Benchmark for Interactive World Models with a Unified Action Generation Framework](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03941v2)
*Jianjie Fang,Yingshan Lei,Qin Wan,Ziyou Wang,Yuchao Huang,Yongyan Xu,Baining Zhao,Weichen Zhang,Chen Gao,Xinlei Chen,Yong Li*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 交互世界模型benchmark与统一动作生成，可评估agent交互能力

TL;DR: 提出iWorld-Bench基准，包含33万视频片段、2,100高质量样本和4,900测试样本，统一评估世界模型在交互任务上的能力，发现现有模型关键限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前缺乏大规模数据集和统一基准来评估世界模型的物理交互能力，阻碍AGI发展。

Method: 构建大规模多样化数据集，引入动作生成框架统一评估不同交互模态，设计六种任务类型生成测试样本。

Result: 评估14个代表性世界模型，识别其关键限制，公开排行榜。

Conclusion: iWorld-Bench为世界模型交互能力评估提供统一标准，揭示现有模型不足，指导未来研究。

中文摘要：实现人工通用智能（AGI）需要能够自适应学习和互动的智能体，其中交互式世界模型为感知、推理和行动提供了可扩展的环境。然而，目前的研究仍缺乏大规模数据集和统一基准来评估其物理交互能力。为解决这一问题，我们提出了iWorld-Bench，一个用于训练和测试世界模型在距离感知和记忆等交互相关能力上的综合基准。我们构建了一个包含33万个视频片段的数据集，并挑选了2,100个高质量样本，涵盖不同的视角、天气和场景。由于现有世界模型在交互模态上有所不同，我们引入了一个动作生成框架以统一评估，并设计了六种任务类型，生成了4,900个测试样本。这些任务共同评估模型在视觉生成、轨迹跟踪和记忆方面的性能。通过评估14个代表性世界模型，我们找出了关键限制，并为未来研究提供了见解。iWorld-Bench模型排行榜可在iWorld-Bench.com上公开获取。

Original abstract: Achieving Artificial General Intelligence (AGI) requires agents that learn and interact adaptively, with interactive world models providing scalable environments for perception, reasoning, and action. Yet current research still lacks large-scale datasets and unified benchmarks to evaluate their physical interaction capabilities. To address this, we propose iWorld-Bench, a comprehensive benchmark for training and testing world models on interaction-related abilities such as distance perception and memory. We construct a diverse dataset with 330k video clips and select 2.1k high-quality samples covering varied perspectives, weather, and scenes. As existing world models differ in interaction modalities, we introduce an Action Generation Framework to unify evaluation and design six task types, generating 4.9k test samples. These tasks jointly assess model performance across visual generation, trajectory following, and memory. Evaluating 14 representative world models, we identify key limitations and provide insights for future research. The iWorld-Bench model leaderboard is publicly available at iWorld-Bench.com.

### [69] [TRACE: A Metrologically-Grounded Engineering Framework for Trustworthy Agentic AI Systems in Operationally Critical Domains](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03838v1)
*Serhii Zabolotnii*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 可信agentic AI工程框架，可迁移的架构与度量

TL;DR: TRACE框架通过四层架构、经典ML与LLM分离、信任度量套件和计算简约比（CPR）实现跨领域可信赖AI，并在三个领域验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 操作关键领域需要可信赖的AI，但现有框架缺乏跨领域通用性和对模型复杂度的量化控制。

Method: 提出四层参考架构，包括L2a/L2b分离、L3策略、L4监督，信任度量套件，以及CPR量化模型简约性。

Result: 在三个不同治理背景的领域（临床、工业、司法）成功应用相同架构和度量。

Conclusion: CPR作为第一类设计原则，将LLM使用从默认转变为有意决策，提升了可信赖性。

中文摘要：我们介绍了TRACE，这是一个用于在操作关键领域中实现可信赖的代理型AI的跨领域工程框架。TRACE结合了四层参考架构，其中包含明确的经典ML与LLM验证器分离（L2a/L2b）、有状态编排与升级策略（L3）以及有限的人类监督（L4）；一套基于计量学的信任度量套件，映射到GUM/VIM/ISO 17025；以及通过计算简约比（CPR）量化的模型简约原则。三个实例——临床决策支持、工业多领域操作和司法AI助手——将相同的架构和度量应用于原则上不同的治理环境。L2a/L2b分离使得大型语言模型的使用成为一种有意的设计决策，而非架构默认，并通过CPR量化简约性。TRACE将CPR作为可信赖AI工程中的一等设计原则引入。

Original abstract: We introduce TRACE, a cross-domain engineering framework for trustworthy agentic AI in operationally critical domains. TRACE combines a four-layer reference architecture with an explicit classical-ML vs. LLM-validator split (L2a/L2b), a stateful orchestration-and-escalation policy (L3), and bounded human supervision (L4); a metrologically grounded trust-metric suite mapped to GUM/VIM/ISO 17025; and a Model-Parsimony principle quantified by the Computational Parsimony Ratio (CPR). Three instantiations--clinical decision support, industrial multi-domain operations, and a judicial AI assistant--transfer the samearchitecture and metrics across principally different governance contexts. The L2a/L2b separation makes the use of large language models a deliberate design decision rather than an architectural default, with parsimony quantified through CPR. TRACE introduces CPR as a first-class design principle in trustworthy-AI engineering.

</details>


### [70] [MCJudgeBench: A Benchmark for Constraint-Level Judge Evaluation in Multi-Constraint Instruction Following](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03858v1)
*Jaeyun Lee,Junyoung Koh,Zeynel Tok,Hunar Batra,Ronald Clark*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 多约束指令跟随评判基准，agent评测方法

TL;DR: 提出了MCJudgeBench基准，用于评估LLM评判者在多约束指令遵循中的约束级别可靠性，发现整体性能好不保证约束级别检测可靠，正确性与不一致性不完全相关，推理提升正确性但非稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估仅关注整体响应判断，忽略了约束级别的可靠性，需要专门的基准来研究LLM评判者的细粒度失败模式。

Method: 构建MCJudgeBench基准，包含指令、候选响应、约束列表、每约束金标签和扰动，设计评估协议包括提示变体，使用正确性和不一致性指标，区分内在和程序不一致性。

Result: 整体性能强的评判者不一定在所有标签类别上可靠，尤其是部分和否类别；高正确性不保证低不一致性；推理提升正确性但未一致提升稳定性。

Conclusion: 应进行约束级别评估以揭示LLM评判者的多维可靠性问题，为改进提供方向。

中文摘要：多约束指令遵循要求验证响应是否满足多个独立需求，然而LLM评判者通常仅通过整体响应判断进行评估。我们引入了MCJudgeBench，这是一个用于多约束指令遵循中约束级别评判者评估的基准。每个实例包含一条指令、一个候选响应、一个显式约束列表、每个约束的金标签（{是，部分，否}）以及受控的响应侧扰动。评估协议进一步包括评估提示变体以测试评判者的稳定性。我们使用正确性和不一致性指标评估了专有和开源的LLM评判者，区分了随机解码下的内在不一致性和提示与响应扰动下的程序不一致性。我们的结果表明，评判者可靠性具有多个维度：强大的整体性能并不能保证在所有标签类别上的检测同样可靠，尤其是对于较罕见的“部分”和“否”案例。正确性更高的评判者并不总是具有更低的不一致性。使用推理进行评估提高了正确性，但并未统一改善稳定性。这些发现促使在约束级别上评估LLM评判者以研究这些失败模式。

Original abstract: Multi-constraint instruction following requires verifying whether a response satisfies multiple individual requirements, yet LLM judges are often assessed only through overall-response judgments. We introduce MCJudgeBench, a benchmark for constraint-level judge evaluation in multi-constraint instruction following. Each instance includes an instruction, a candidate response, an explicit constraint list, per-constraint gold labels in {yes, partial, no}, and controlled response-side perturbations. The evaluation protocol further includes evaluation prompt variants to test judge stability. We evaluate proprietary and open-source LLM judges using both correctness and inconsistency metrics, distinguishing intrinsic inconsistency under stochastic decoding from procedural inconsistency under prompt and response perturbations. Our results show that judge reliability has multiple dimensions: strong overall performance does not guarantee equally reliable detection across label categories, especially for rarer partial and no cases. Judges with higher correctness do not always have lower inconsistency. Evaluation with reasoning improves correctness but does not uniformly improve stability. These findings motivate evaluating LLM judges at the constraint level to study these failure modes.

</details>


### [71] [Safety and accuracy follow different scaling laws in clinical large language models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04039v1)
*Sebastian Wind,Tri-Thien Nguyen,Jeta Sopa,Mahshad Lotfinia,Sebastian Bickelhaup,Michael Uder,Harald Köstler,Gerhard Wellein,Sven Nebelung,Daniel Truhn,Andreas Maier,Soroosh Tayebi Arasteh*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 研究临床LLM安全与准确性的缩放规律，涉及agentic RAG，对agent安全评估有潜在参考。

TL;DR: 临床LLM安全性并非随扩展而自动提升，而是依赖于证据质量、检索设计和上下文构建等部署因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有假设认为更高的准确性意味着更安全，但医学中少数高风险错误比平均性能更重要，因此需要系统评估安全性如何随各种扩展维度变化。

Method: 提出SaFE-Scale框架和RadSaFE-200基准，在六种部署条件下评估34个LLM的安全性能。

Result: 干净证据大幅提升准确率并降低风险指标，而RAG和最大上下文未能复制安全性改善，额外推理计算收益有限，错误集中在少数问题上。

Conclusion: 临床LLM安全性是部署特性而非扩展的被动结果，需要关注证据质量、检索设计和错误集中行为。

中文摘要：临床大语言模型（LLMs）通常通过增加模型大小、上下文长度、检索复杂性或推理计算来扩展，其隐含期望是更高的准确性意味着更安全的行为。这一假设在医学中是不完整的，因为少数几个自信的、高风险的或与证据相矛盾的错误可能比平均基准性能更重要。我们引入了SaFE-Scale，一个用于测量临床LLM安全性如何随模型规模、证据质量、检索策略、上下文暴露和推理计算变化的框架。为了实例化这一框架，我们引入了RadSaFE-200，一个放射学安全聚焦评估基准，包含200道多项选择题，具有临床医生定义的干净证据、冲突证据以及高风险错误、不安全答案和证据矛盾的选项级别标签。我们评估了34个本地部署的LLM在六种部署条件下：闭书提示（零样本）、干净证据、冲突证据、标准RAG、代理RAG和最大上下文提示。干净证据产生了最大的改进，平均准确率从73.5%提高到94.1%，同时高风险错误从12.0%降至2.6%，矛盾从12.7%降至2.3%，危险过度自信从8.0%降至1.6%。标准RAG和代理RAG没有复制这种安全特性：代理RAG比标准RAG提高了准确率并减少了矛盾，但高风险错误和危险过度自信仍然较高。最大上下文提示增加了延迟但没有缩小安全差距，额外的推理计算只产生了有限的收益。最坏情况分析显示，临床重要错误集中在一小部分问题上。因此，临床LLM安全性不是扩展的被动结果，而是受证据质量、检索设计、上下文构建和集体失败行为影响的部署特性。

Original abstract: Clinical LLMs are often scaled by increasing model size, context length, retrieval complexity, or inference-time compute, with the implicit expectation that higher accuracy implies safer behavior. This assumption is incomplete in medicine, where a few confident, high-risk, or evidence-contradicting errors can matter more than average benchmark performance. We introduce SaFE-Scale, a framework for measuring how clinical LLM safety changes across model scale, evidence quality, retrieval strategy, context exposure, and inference-time compute. To instantiate this framework, we introduce RadSaFE-200, a Radiology Safety-Focused Evaluation benchmark of 200 multiple-choice questions with clinician-defined clean evidence, conflict evidence, and option-level labels for high-risk error, unsafe answer, and evidence contradiction. We evaluated 34 locally deployed LLMs across six deployment conditions: closed-book prompting (zero-shot), clean evidence, conflict evidence, standard RAG, agentic RAG, and max-context prompting. Clean evidence produced the strongest improvement, increasing mean accuracy from 73.5% to 94.1%, while reducing high-risk error from 12.0% to 2.6%, contradiction from 12.7% to 2.3%, and dangerous overconfidence from 8.0% to 1.6%. Standard RAG and agentic RAG did not reproduce this safety profile: agentic RAG improved accuracy over standard RAG and reduced contradiction, but high-risk error and dangerous overconfidence remained elevated. Max-context prompting increased latency without closing the safety gap, and additional inference-time compute produced only limited gains. Worst-case analysis showed that clinically consequential errors concentrated in a small subset of questions. Clinical LLM safety is therefore not a passive consequence of scaling, but a deployment property shaped by evidence quality, retrieval design, context construction, and collective failure behavior.

</details>


### [72] [NoisyCausal: A Benchmark for Evaluating Causal Reasoning Under Structured Noise](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04313v1)
*Zhi Xu,Yun Fu*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 因果推理框架结合LLM与符号结构，可迁移agent推理

TL;DR: 提出NoisyCausal基准和模块化推理框架，通过显式因果结构引导LLM，显著提升因果推理鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLMs在噪声条件下难以区分相关性和因果关系，现有方法缺乏对结构化噪声的鲁棒性。

Method: 构建NoisyCausal基准，包含可控噪声的因果推理实例；提出模块化框架，引导LLM提取变量、构建因果图并进行结构化推理。

Result: 在NoisyCausal和Cladder上，该方法显著优于标准提示和推理基线，且无需任务特定调优。

Conclusion: 结合因果抽象与语言驱动推理对于实现LLMs中忠实和鲁棒的因果理解至关重要。

中文摘要：自然语言中的因果推理需要识别相关变量，理解它们的交互，并在噪声或模糊条件下推理效果和干预措施。尽管大型语言模型（LLMs）展现出强大的通用推理能力，但它们难以区分相关性和因果关系，尤其是在观察结果部分错误或存在无关信息的情况下。在这项工作中，我们引入了NoisyCausal，这是一个新的基准，旨在评估结构化噪声下的因果推理。每个实例都从真实因果图生成，并通过注入可控形式的噪声（如无关干扰项、值扰动、混杂和部分可观测性）将其情境化为自然语言场景。此外，我们提出了一个模块化推理框架，将LLMs与显式因果结构相结合以应对这些挑战。我们的方法提示LLM提取变量，从上下文中构建因果图，然后将推理任务重新表述为基于该图的结构化提示。LLM在符号结构的引导下，而非仅依赖统计模式，从而实现更可解释和鲁棒的推理。实验结果表明，我们的方法在NoisyCausal上显著优于标准提示和推理基线。此外，它在外部基准（如Cladder）上也能很好地泛化，无需任务特定调优。我们的发现强调了将因果抽象与语言驱动推理相结合以实现LLMs中忠实和鲁棒的因果理解的重要性。

Original abstract: Causal reasoning in natural language requires identifying relevant variables, understanding their interactions, and reasoning about effects and interventions, often under noisy or ambiguous conditions. While large language models (LLMs) exhibit strong general reasoning abilities, they struggle to disentangle correlation from causation, particularly when observations are partially incorrect or irrelevant information is present. In this work, we introduce NoisyCausal, a new benchmark designed to evaluate causal reasoning under structured noise. Each instance is generated from a ground-truth causal graph and contextualized with a natural language scenario by injecting controllable forms of noise, such as irrelevant distractors, value perturbations, confounding, and partial observability. Moreover, we propose a modular reasoning framework that combines LLMs with explicit causal structure to address these challenges. Our method prompts the LLM to extract variables, construct a causal graph from context, and then reformulates the reasoning task as a structured prompt grounded in this graph. Rather than relying on statistical patterns alone, the LLM is guided by symbolic structure, enabling more interpretable and robust inference. Experimental results show that our method significantly outperforms standard prompting and reasoning baselines on NoisyCausal. Furthermore, it generalizes well to external benchmarks such as Cladder without task-specific tuning. Our findings highlight the importance of combining causal abstractions with language-driven reasoning to achieve faithful and robust causal understanding in LLMs.

### [73] [Physics-Grounded Multi-Agent Architecture for Traceable, Risk-Aware Human-AI Decision Support in Manufacturing](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04003v1)
*Danny Hoang,Ryan Matthiessen,Christopher Miller,Nasir Mannan,Ruby ElKharboutly,David Gorsich,Matthew P. Castanier,Farhad Imani*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: 提出多agent知识分析架构用于制造决策，含批判与验证，通用多agent协作方法可迁移。

TL;DR: MAKA是一种多代理人在回路决策支持架构，通过结合LLM推理与专用工具及验证，将工具执行成功率提升高达87.5%，并将表面偏差降至±10^{-3}英寸。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现成LLM无法可靠执行风险约束的多步骤数值工作流或提供高风险决策的可审计来源。

Method: 提出MAKA架构，分离意图路由、定量分析、知识图谱检索和评论家验证；在Ti-6Al-4V转子叶片试验台上通过融合虚拟加工、力仿真和3D检测数据实例化，将偏差分解为路径、磨损、柔度和变异性分量。

Result: 在三层基准测试中，MAKA将成功工具执行率提高高达87.5个百分点；数字孪生仿真显示预测表面偏差从10^{-2}英寸降至约±10^{-3}英寸。

Conclusion: MAKA实现了可追溯、风险感知的加工补偿，为人类决策提供部署前验证信号。

中文摘要：高精度CNC加工自由形态航空航天部件需要基于检测、仿真和工艺知识的有界补偿。现成的大型语言模型（LLM）助手能够生成文本，但无法可靠地执行受风险约束的多步骤数值工作流，也无法为高风险决策提供可审计的来源。我们提出了多代理知识分析（MAKA），一种人在回路的决策支持架构，它将意图路由、仅工具定量分析、知识图谱检索和基于评论家的验证分离，在推荐提交人工批准之前强制执行物理合理性、安全边界和来源完整性。MAKA在Ti-6Al-4V转子叶片加工试验台上实例化，融合了虚拟加工路径跟踪误差场、切削力和变形仿真，以及来自16个叶片的基于扫描的三维检测偏差图。该分析将偏差分解为证据关联的路径分量、漂移基磨损代理（捕捉零件间的系统演变）、残余系统柔度项以及用于感知不稳定性升级的变异性代理。在三层工具编排基准测试中（从单步到≥3步有状态序列），与具有相同工具访问权限的非结构化单模型交互模式相比，MAKA将成功工具执行率提高了高达87.5个百分点。数字孪生假设分析表明，MAKA能够协调可追溯的补偿候选方案，在仿真环境中将大部分叶片表面的预测偏差从10^{-2}英寸量级降低到约±10^{-3}英寸，为风险意识的人类决策提供了部署前验证信号。

Original abstract: High-precision CNC machining of free-form aerospace components requires bounded compensations informed by inspection, simulation, and process knowledge. Off-the-shelf large language model (LLM) assistants can generate text, but they do not reliably execute risk-constrained multi-step numerical workflows or provide auditable provenance for high-stakes decisions. We present multi-agent knowledge analysis (MAKA), a human-in-the-loop decision-support architecture that separates intent routing, tools-only quantitative analysis, knowledge graph retrieval, and critic-based verification that enforces physical plausibility, safety bounds, and provenance completeness before recommendations are surfaced for human approval. MAKA is instantiated on a Ti-6Al-4V rotor blade machining testbed by fusing virtual-machining path-tracking error fields, cutting-force and deflection simulations, and scan-based 3D inspection deviation maps from 16 blades. The analysis decomposes deviation into an evidence-linked pathing component, a drift-based wear proxy capturing systematic evolution across parts, a residual systematic compliance term, and a variability proxy for instability-aware escalation. In a three-level tool-orchestration benchmark (single-step through $\geq$3-step stateful sequences), MAKA improves successful tool execution by up to 87.5 percentage points relative to an unstructured single-model interaction pattern with identical tool access. Digital twin what-if studies show MAKA can coordinate traceable compensation candidates that reduce predicted surface deviation from order $10^{-2}$in to approximately $\pm 10^{-3}$in over most of the blade within the simulation environment, providing a pre-deployment verification signal for risk-aware human decision-making.

### [74] [ARMATA: Auto-Regressive Multi-Agent Task Assignment](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04225v1)
*Yazan Youssef,Aboelmagd Noureldin,Sidney Givigi*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: 多智能体任务分配框架，可迁移至多agent协作与规划

TL;DR: 提出集中式端到端自回归框架联合求解多智能体任务分配和路径规划，多阶段解码机制统一分配与路由，显著优于工业求解器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法将分配和路径解耦或使用分散式启发式，忽略阶段间依赖且缺乏全局视角，导致局部最优和效率低下。

Method: 提出集中式端到端自回归框架，采用多阶段解码机制，在单个自回归过程中联合生成高层的分配决策和低层的路径序列，并维护中央全局状态。

Result: 在多个基准上比Google OR-Tools、IBM CPLEX和LKH-3等工业求解器提升高达20%的解质量，计算时间从小时级降至秒级。

Conclusion: 该端到端方法有效平衡工作负载和路径效率，避免局部最优，具有显著的实际应用价值。

中文摘要：协调分布在空间区域的多智能体系统需要解决一个复杂的层次问题：首先在各智能体之间分配区域（分配），然后确定最优访问顺序（路径规划）。现有方法通常将这两个阶段解耦，忽略了阶段间的依赖关系，或依赖于缺乏全局视角的分散式启发式方法。在这项工作中，我们提出了一种集中式的、完全端到端的自回归框架，该框架联合生成分配决策和路径序列。我们方法的核心贡献是一种多阶段解码机制，该机制在单个自回归过程中统一了高层分配和低层路径规划，同时维护集中的全局状态。这使得模型能够隐式地平衡工作负载分配与路径效率，避免了分散式方法中常见的局部最优。大量实验表明，我们的方法显著优于各种基线，在解决方案质量上比Google OR-Tools、IBM CPLEX和LKH-3等工业求解器提高了多达20%，同时将计算时间从数小时减少到数秒。

Original abstract: Coordinating multi-agent systems over spatially distributed areas requires solving a complex hierarchical problem: first distributing areas among agents (allocation) and subsequently determining the optimal visitation order (routing). Existing methods typically decouple these stages ignoring inter-stage dependencies or rely on decentralized heuristics that lack global context. In this work, we propose a centralized, fully end-to-end auto-regressive framework that jointly generates allocation decisions and routing sequences. The core contribution of our approach is a multi-stage decoding mechanism that unifies high-level allocation and low-level routing in a single autoregressive pass while maintaining a centralized global state. This enables the model to implicitly balance workload distribution with routing efficiency, avoiding local optima common in decentralized methods. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our method significantly outperforms diverse baselines, achieving up to a 20\% improvement in solution quality over industrial solvers such as Google OR-Tools, IBM CPLEX, and LKH-3, while reducing computation time from hours to seconds.

### [75] [A Skill-Based AI Agentic Pipeline for Library of Congress Subject Indexing](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03537v1)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Original abstract: This paper presents a modular AI agentic skill pipeline for automating subject indexing with Library of Congress Subject Headings (LCSH). Subject indexing - the process of analyzing a work's aboutness, selecting controlled vocabulary terms, and encoding them as MARC21 subject access fields - is one of the most time-consuming components of library cataloging. The system decomposes this process into four discrete, sequentially executed agent skills: conceptual analysis, quantitative filtering, authority validation, and MARC field synthesis. Each skill encodes domain knowledge drawn directly from Library of Congress Subject Headings Manual (SHM) instruction sheets and subject analysis theory. The pipeline was evaluated against a corpus of ten titles whose existing subject headings were captured from the Harvard Library bibliographic dataset (a snapshot of their Alma ILS). Results demonstrate strong conceptual alignment with professional subject indexing practice, with notable differences in specificity, subdivision practice, and the agent's adherence to the 2026 LC policy discontinuing form subdivisions in favor of LCGFT 655 fields.

### [76] [Cryptographic Registry Provenance: Structural Defense Against Dependency Confusion in AI Package Ecosystems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03309v2)
*Alan L. McCann*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出一种基于双重签名和注册表身份的密码学分发溯源系统，可防御依赖混淆攻击，并在八个生态系统中验证其缺失性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有依赖混淆攻击防御均为配置驱动且静默失效，缺乏密码学保证。

Method: 构建包含注册表身份（Ed25519密钥对）、双重签名模型（发布者签名+注册表副署）和命名空间绑定（消费者指纹固定+密码学拒绝）的三层系统。

Result: 在npm等八个生态系统中均未发现同时实现所有三层防御的系统；系统可扩展至AI溯源并集成运行时治理。

Conclusion: 该系统通过密码学方法填补了软件分发中的信任缺口，为依赖混淆攻击提供了根本性防御。

中文摘要：依赖混淆攻击利用了软件分发中的结构性缺陷：一旦安装了某个包，就没有密码学证据证明是哪个注册表分发了它。现有的每种防御都是基于配置的，并且在配置错误时会静默失败。我们提出了一个密码学分发溯源系统，包含三个组件：（1）密码学注册表身份，其中每个注册表持有一个Ed25519密钥对并对它分发的每个工件签名；（2）双重签名模型，发布者在打包时签名，注册表在发布时进行副署签名；（3）权威命名空间绑定，消费者固定注册表指纹，解析器在密码学上拒绝来自未授权注册表的工件。这些创建了三层防御，成功攻击需要同时攻破所有三层。对八个生态系统（npm、Cargo、Hex.pm、PyPI、Go模块、Docker/OCI、NuGet、Maven）的比较显示，现有生态系统没有将强制发布者签名、密码学注册表身份、强制注册表副署签名和消费者端密码学强制执行结合起来。该系统扩展至AI生成溯源，作为签名属性和治理强制依赖解析。一个案例研究将分发溯源与一个三层运行时治理架构集成，创建了一个没有密码学漏洞的四阶段生命周期链。

Original abstract: Dependency confusion attacks exploit a structural gap in software distribution: once a package is installed, there is no cryptographic proof of which registry distributed it. Every existing defense is configuration-based and fails silently when misconfigured. We present a cryptographic distribution provenance system comprising three components: (1) cryptographic registry identity, where every registry holds an Ed25519 keypair and signs every artifact it distributes; (2) a dual-signature model, where the publisher signs at packaging time and the registry countersigns at publication time; and (3) authoritative namespace binding, where consumers pin registry fingerprints and the resolver cryptographically rejects artifacts from unauthorized registries. These create three defense layers requiring simultaneous compromise for a successful attack. A comparison across eight ecosystems (npm, Cargo, Hex.pm, PyPI, Go modules, Docker/OCI, NuGet, Maven) shows no existing ecosystem combines mandatory publisher signing, cryptographic registry identity, mandatory registry countersigning, and consumer-side cryptographic enforcement. The system extends to AI-generation provenance as a signed attribute and governance-enforced dependency resolution. A case study integrates distribution provenance with a three-layer runtime governance architecture, creating a four-phase lifecycle chain with no cryptographic gaps.

</details>


### [77] [SkCC: Portable and Secure Skill Compilation for Cross-Framework LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03353v4)
*Yipeng Ouyang,Yi Xiao,Yuhao Gu,Xianwei Zhang*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: SkCC提出跨框架agent技能编译，直接针对coding agent的便携性与安全性。

TL;DR: SkCC是一个LLM智能体技能编译器，通过强类型中间表示SkIR解耦技能语义与框架格式，并引入静态优化器保证安全，显著提升可移植性和性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM智能体技能缺乏可移植性，框架对格式敏感导致性能差异大，且需要为每个框架重写，同时安全性未得到解决，存在广泛漏洞。

Method: 提出SkCC编译器，包含四阶段流水线：基于强类型中间表示SkIR解耦语义与格式，静态优化器在部署前强制安全约束，从而将适应复杂度从O(m×n)降至O(m+n)。

Result: 在SkillsBench上，Claude Code通过率从21.1%提升至33.3%，Kimi CLI从35.1%提升至48.7%；编译延迟<10ms，主动安全触发率94.8%，运行时token节省10-46%。

Conclusion: SkCC有效解决了技能可移植性和安全性问题，降低了适配成本，提升了性能，具有实际应用价值。

中文摘要：LLM智能体越来越依赖可复用技能（例如，SKILL markdown文件）来执行复杂任务，然而这些制品缺乏可移植性：智能体框架对提示词格式高度敏感，导致同一技能的性能差异很大。尽管如此，大多数技能仅以格式无关的Markdown一次性编写，这需要为每个框架进行昂贵的重写，并且安全性也基本未得到解决，在实践中存在广泛漏洞。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了SkCC，一个用于LLM智能体的编译器，它将经典编译设计引入智能体技能开发。SkCC以SkIR为核心，这是一种强类型中间表示，它将技能语义与特定框架的格式解耦，从而实现了跨智能体框架的可移植部署。在该IR之上，静态优化器强制安全约束，在部署前阻止漏洞。作为四阶段流水线实现，SkCC有效地将适应复杂度从O(m×n)降低到O(m+n)（m个技能，n个框架）。在SkillsBench上的实验表明，SkCC比原始对应物取得了持续且显著的改进，在Claude Code上通过率从21.1%提高到33.3%，在Kimi CLI上从35.1%提高到48.7%。此外，该设计实现了亚10毫秒的编译延迟、94.8%的主动安全触发率以及跨框架10-46%的运行时代币节省。

Original abstract: LLM agents increasingly rely on reusable skills (e.g., SKILL markdown files) to execute complex tasks, yet these artifacts lack portability: agent frameworks are highly sensitive to prompt formatting, leading to a large performance variation for the same skill. Nevertheless, most skills are authored once as format-agnostic Markdown, necessitating costly per-framework rewrites and also leaving security largely unaddressed, with widespread vulnerabilities in practice. To address this, we present SkCC, a compiler for LLM agents that introduces classical compilation design into agent skill development. SkCC centers on SkIR, a strongly-typed intermediate representation that decouples skill semantics from framework-specific formatting, thus enabling portable deployment across agent frameworks. Atop of this IR, a static Optimizer enforces security constraints, blocking vulnerabilities before deployment. Implemented as a four-phase pipeline, SkCC effectively reduces adaptation complexity from $O(m \times n)$ to $O(m + n)$ across $m$ skills and $n$ frameworks. Experiments on SkillsBench demonstrate that SkCC delivers consistent and substantial gains over original counterparts, with pass rate increases from 21.1% to 33.3% on Claude Code and from 35.1% to 48.7% on Kimi CLI. Further, the design achieves sub-10ms compilation latency, 94.8% proactive security trigger rate, and 10-46% runtime token savings across frameworks.

### [78] [ARGUS: Defending LLM Agents Against Context-Aware Prompt Injection](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03378v2)
*Shihao Weng,Yang Feng,Jinrui Zhang,Xiaofei Xie,Jiongchi Yu,Jia Liu*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出AgentLure基准和ARGUS防御，通过因果溯源审计有效降低上下文感知提示注入的攻击成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准和防御无法应对上下文感知提示注入，导致代理在上下文依赖任务中易受攻击。

Method: 构建AgentLure基准（覆盖四个代理领域、八个攻击向量和六个攻击面），提出ARGUS因果溯源审计器，通过构建影响溯源图、标记运行时跨度、将动作参数基于支持证据，仅在良性证据蕴含且任务不变性保持时释放动作。

Result: 在AgentLure上，ARGUS将攻击成功率从28.8%降至3.8%，同时保留87.5%的清洁效用。

Conclusion: ARGUS在安全-效用权衡中显著优于现有防御，为LLM代理提供了有效的上下文感知提示注入防护。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）代理越来越多地被部署为面向任务的软件系统，这些系统利用运行时上下文来决定并代表用户行动。这种委托模式使得提示注入尤其危险：攻击者可以在代理必须用来决定做什么的证据中隐藏一个上下文感知的指令。现有的基准和防御措施大多忽略了这种场景。基准通常使用上下文无关的任务，其中用户提示已经指定了预期的动作，同时结合与上下文无关的通用攻击载荷。现有的防御措施也没有捕捉从运行时证据到具体动作的因果支持，这使得它们对于上下文依赖的任务是不完整且无效的。我们提出了AgentLure，一个针对上下文感知提示注入的上下文依赖任务的基准。AgentLure涵盖四个代理领域和八个攻击向量，跨越六个攻击面。为了防御这种场景，我们提出了ARGUS，一种用于LLM代理的因果溯源审计器。不是仅依赖于工具授权或可疑上下文检测，ARGUS验证每个提议的动作是否具有完整的良性因果证明。它构建了一个影响溯源图，标记运行时跨度，将动作参数基于支持证据，并且仅在良性证据蕴含动作且任务不变性保持时释放动作。在AgentLure上，ARGUS将攻击成功率从28.8%降低到3.8%，同时保留了87.5%的清洁效用，在安全-效用权衡中显著优于现有防御。

Original abstract: Large Language Model (LLM) agents are increasingly deployed as task-oriented software systems that use runtime context to decide and act on behalf of users. This delegation model makes prompt injection especially dangerous: an attacker can hide a context-aware instruction inside evidence the agent must use to decide what to do. Existing benchmarks and defenses largely miss this setting. Benchmarks often use context-insensitive tasks where the user prompt already specifies the intended action, together with generic attack payloads independent of context. Existing defenses also do not capture the causal support from runtime evidence to concrete actions, which makes them incomplete and ineffective for context-dependent tasks.
  We present AgentLure, a benchmark for context-dependent tasks under context-aware prompt injection. AgentLure spans four agentic domains and eight attack vectors across six attack surfaces. To defend this setting, we propose ARGUS, a causal-provenance auditor for LLM agents. Instead of relying only on tool authorization or suspicious-context detection, ARGUS verifies whether each proposed action has a complete benign causal justification. It builds an influence-provenance graph, labels runtime spans, grounds action arguments in supporting evidence, and releases an action only when benign evidence entails it and task invariants hold. On AgentLure, ARGUS reduces attack success rate from 28.8% to 3.8% while preserving 87.5% clean utility, significantly outperforming existing defenses in the security-utility tradeoff.

</details>


### [79] [MEMSAD: Gradient-Coupled Anomaly Detection for Memory Poisoning in Retrieval-Augmented Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03482v2)
*Ishrith Gowda*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: MEMSAD对检索增强agent的内存投毒攻击进行形式化分析与防御，直接涉及agent安全与鲁棒性。

TL;DR: 本文形式化记忆投毒攻击，提出MEMSAD防御（基于梯度耦合定理的校准检测），理论达到极小极大最优，实验显示复合防御完美检测，但同义词替换攻击仍可逃避。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM代理的记忆投毒攻击缺乏形式化安全分析和统一评估，现有评估协议存在不一致性，需要理论保证的防御方法。

Method: 将攻击形式化为Stackelberg博弈，构建三类攻击的统一框架；提出MEMSAD，基于梯度耦合定理（异常分数与检索目标梯度一致）设计校准检测，并证明其极小极大最优性和在线遗憾界。

Result: 修正评估后ASR-R提升4倍（0.25→1.00）；MEMSAD提供认证检测半径；复合防御在全部攻击上TPR=1.00，FPR=0.00；但同义词替换攻击在Δ ASR-R≈0时完美逃避。

Conclusion: 提供了记忆安全的形式化理论和有效防御，同时暴露了连续空间防御的离散攻击漏洞，需进一步研究应对同义词等离散扰动。

中文摘要：持久性外部记忆使得LLM代理能够在会话之间维持上下文，但其安全属性尚未得到正式刻画。我们将针对检索增强代理的记忆投毒攻击形式化为一个Stackelberg博弈，并构建一个统一的评估框架，涵盖三种攻击类别，其访问假设逐步升级。修正了Chen等人（2024）在触发查询规范中的评估协议不一致问题，我们表明忠实评估使得测量到的攻击成功率提高了4倍（ASR-R: 0.25 → 1.00）。我们的主要贡献是MEMSAD（语义异常检测），一种基于校准的防御方法，建立在梯度耦合定理之上：在编码器正则性条件下，异常分数梯度与检索目标梯度被证明是相同的，因此任何降低检测风险的连续扰动必然降低检索排名。这种耦合产生了一个认证的检测半径，无论对手策略如何，都能保证正确分类。我们通过Le Cam方法证明了极小极大最优性，表明任何阈值检测器需要Ω(1/ρ^2)个校准样本，而MEMSAD在log(1/δ)因子内达到该下界。我们进一步推导了滚动校准的在线遗憾界，速率为O(σ^{2/3}Δ^{1/3})，并正式刻画了一个离散的同义词不变性漏洞，标志着连续空间防御所能保证的边界。在3×5攻击-防御矩阵上的实验，结合bootstrap置信区间、Bonferroni校正假设检验和Clopper-Pearson验证（n=1000），确认：复合防御在所有攻击上实现了TPR=1.00，FPR=0.00，而同义词替换在Δ ASR-R≈0时逃避检测，暴露了现有基于嵌入的防御无法弥补的差距。

Original abstract: Persistent external memory enables LLM agents to maintain context across sessions, yet its security properties remain formally uncharacterized. We formalize memory poisoning attacks on retrieval-augmented agents as a Stackelberg game with a unified evaluation framework spanning three attack classes with escalating access assumptions. Correcting an evaluation protocol inconsistency in the triggered-query specification of Chen et al. (2024), we show faithful evaluation increases measured attack success by $4\times$ (ASR-R: $0.25 \to 1.00$). Our primary contribution is MEMSAD (Semantic Anomaly Detection), a calibration-based defense grounded in a gradient coupling theorem: under encoder regularity, the anomaly score gradient and the retrieval objective gradient are provably identical, so any continuous perturbation that reduces detection risk necessarily degrades retrieval rank. This coupling yields a certified detection radius guaranteeing correct classification regardless of adversary strategy. We prove minimax optimality via Le Cam's method, showing any threshold detector requires $Ω(1/ρ^2)$ calibration samples and MEMSAD achieves this up to $\log(1/δ)$ factors. We further derive online regret bounds for rolling calibration at rate $O(σ^{2/3}Δ^{1/3})$, and formally characterize a discrete synonym-invariance loophole that marks the boundary of what continuous-space defenses can guarantee. Experiments on a $3 \times 5$ attack-defense matrix with bootstrap confidence intervals, Bonferroni-corrected hypothesis tests, and Clopper-Pearson validation ($n=1{,}000$) confirm: composite defenses achieve TPR $= 1.00$, FPR $= 0.00$ across all attacks, while synonym substitution evades detection at $Δ$ ASR-R $\approx 0$, exposing a gap existing embedding-based defenses cannot close.

</details>


### [80] [From TinyGo to gc Compiler: Extending Zorya's Concolic Framework to Real-World Go Binaries](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03492v2)
*Karolina Gorna,Nicolas Iooss,Yannick Seurin,Rida Khatoun,Keith Makan*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: Zorya扩展至多线程Go二进制文件，检测静默漏洞，在11个真实漏洞中发现7个。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前版本仅支持单线程TinyGo二进制文件，需要扩展支持Go标准gc编译器生成的多线程二进制文件。

Method: 通过从gdb转储恢复OS线程状态、消除运行时抢占，以及引入带有写时复制语义的覆盖路径分析，检测未采用分支上的静默漏洞。

Result: 在11个真实世界漏洞（来自Kubernetes、Go-Ethereum、CoreDNS）上评估，检测到7个二进制级漏洞，包括一个静默整数溢出，其他工具在没有手动编写预言时无法检测。

Conclusion: Zorya有效检测多线程Go二进制文件中的漏洞，能发现其他工具遗漏的静默漏洞。

中文摘要：Zorya是一个混合执行框架，它将编译后的二进制文件提升到Ghidra的P-Code中间表示，并使用Z3 SMT求解器通过推理具体值和符号值来检测漏洞。之前的版本只支持单线程的TinyGo二进制文件。在本文中，我们将Zorya扩展到由Go标准gc编译器生成的多线程二进制文件。这是通过从gdb转储恢复OS线程状态、消除运行时抢占以及引入带有写时复制语义的覆盖路径分析来检测未采用分支上的静默漏洞实现的。我们在来自生产级Go项目（如Kubernetes、Go-Ethereum和CoreDNS）的11个真实世界漏洞上严格评估了Zorya。我们的评估表明，Zorya在二进制级别检测到7个漏洞，包括一个静默整数溢出，而其他评估工具在没有手动编写预言的情况下无法检测到。

Original abstract: Zorya is a concolic execution framework that lifts compiled binaries to Ghidra's P-Code intermediate representation and uses the Z3 SMT solver to detect vulnerabilities by reasoning over both concrete and symbolic values. Previous versions supported only single-threaded TinyGo binaries. In this paper, we extend Zorya to multi-threaded binaries produced by Go's standard gc compiler. This is achieved by restoring OS thread states from gdb dumps, neutralizing runtime preemption, and introducing overlay path analysis with copy-on-write semantics to detect silent vulnerabilities on untaken branches. We rigorously assess Zorya on 11 real-world vulnerabilities from production Go projects such as Kubernetes, Go-Ethereum, and CoreDNS. Our evaluation shows that Zorya detects seven bugs at the binary level, including a silent integer overflow detects no other evaluated tool finds without a manually written oracle.

In this paper, we present an LLM-based framework for practical smart contract vulnerability detection. We construct and release a large-scale dataset comprising 31,165 professionally annotated vulnerability instances collected from over 3,200 real-world projects across 15 major blockchain platforms. Our approach leverages precise AST-based context extraction and vulnerability-specific prompt design to instantiate customized detectors for 13 prevalent vulnerability categories. ### [82] [Firmware Distribution as Attack Surface: A Security Study of ASIC Cryptocurrency Miners](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03770v2)
*Pierre Pouliquen,Hadrien Barral,David Naccache,Thibaut Heckmann,Antoine Houssais*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 通过静态分析公开发布的固件工件，揭示了ASIC矿机固件分发生态中的安全漏洞和大规模攻击可能性。

Method: 基于收集和静态分析公开发布的固件工件，无需设备访问或运行时交互，重建并分析134个固件镜像。

Original abstract: ASIC cryptocurrency miners are a core component of blockchain infrastructures, directly converting computation and energy into monetary value. Despite their economic importance, their security is rarely evaluated in a structured manner. In this paper, we show that the firmware distribution ecosystem of mining devices fundamentally challenges existing trust assumptions. We introduce a scalable methodology based on the collection and static analysis of publicly distributed firmware artifacts, requiring neither device access nor runtime interaction. Applying this approach, we reconstruct and analyze 134 firmware images spanning manufacturers that account for over 99% of deployed miners (Bitmain, MicroBT, Canaan, Iceriver). Our results reveal that firmware artifacts alone are sufficient to recover internal architecture, identify security weaknesses, and reconstruct complete attack paths leading to high-impact adversarial objectives. In particular, our analysis reveals vulnerabilities that enable realistic large-scale attack scenarios, including firmware phishing and the exploitation of miners still operating over Stratum V1. Validation on two real devices confirms that publicly distributed artifacts closely reflect deployed software and that these weaknesses translate into attack capabilities. Overall, our study shows that firmware distribution mechanisms themselves constitute a primary attack surface, significantly lowering the barrier to compromise in the ASIC mining ecosystem.

### [83] [MOSAIC-Bench: Measuring Compositional Vulnerability Induction in Coding Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03952v1)
*Jonathan Steinberg,Oren Gal*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出MOSAIC-Bench基准测试，展示编码助手在面对序列化无害工单时生成可利用代码的高成功率（53-86%），而直接提示时防御有效；下游审查者批准了25.8%的易受攻击代码。重新定义审查者为对抗性渗透测试者可将规避率降至3.0-17.6%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有安全对齐方法仅孤立评估明确请求，忽略了模型在顺序执行多个看似无害的工单时可能组合出恶意结果的问题，导致编码助手在分解任务时产生安全漏洞。

Method: 构建MOSAIC-Bench，包含199个三阶段攻击链，使用10个Web应用基板、31个CWE类别和5种编程语言，评估9个生产编码助手和4个前沿模型。比较直接提示与工单编排场景，并测试不同下游审查者协议及对抗性渗透测试框架。

Result: 工单编排下，编码助手端到端ASR为53-86%，仅两次拒绝；直接提示下，易受攻击输出率降至0-20.4%。下游审查者批准25.8%的易受攻击代码。对抗性渗透测试框架将规避率降至3.0-17.6%，最佳审查者检测率为88.4%，误报率4.6%。

Conclusion: 编码助手的安全问题本质上是结构性的，工单编排能同时绕过直接提示下的拒绝和硬化防御。将代码审查者重新构建为对抗性渗透测试者是一种有效的非自适应缓解措施，但需要进一步研究自适应防御。

中文摘要：编码助手通常能够通过逐提示的安全审查，但当其任务被分解为常规工程工单时，却会交付可被利用的代码。挑战在于结构性：现有的安全对齐方法孤立地评估明确的请求，使得模型对源于对看似无害的请求的顺序遵从而产生的恶意最终状态视而不见。我们引入了MOSAIC-Bench（恶意目标通过无害遵从序列化），这是一个包含199个三阶段攻击链的基准测试，并配有在已部署软件基板（10个Web应用基板、31个CWE类别、5种编程语言）上的确定性利用预言机，该基准将利用真实情况和下游审查者协议作为第一类评估轴。在该基准上，来自Anthropic、OpenAI、Google、Moonshot、Zhipu和Minimax的九个生产编码助手以53-86%的端到端攻击成功率（ASR）编排无害工单，在所有分阶段运行中仅出现两次拒绝。在针对四个前沿Claude/Codex助手的匹配直接提示实验中，易受攻击输出率降至0-20.4%：Claude主要拒绝，而Codex主要硬化而非发出易受攻击的实现——工单编排同时沉默了这两种防御模式。在下游，代码审查者批准了这些已确认易受攻击的累积差异中的25.8%作为常规PR，而全上下文实现协议仅关闭了编排/直接差距的50%，排除了上下文碎片作为唯一解释。作为一种可部署但非自适应的缓解措施，将审查者重新定义为对抗性渗透测试者，在所评估的审查者子集上降低了规避率；渗透测试框架下的规避率范围为3.0%至17.6%，而在此框架下，一个开放权重的Gemma-4-E4B-it审查者在数据集上检测到88.4%的攻击，误报率为4.6%（在608个真实世界GitHub PR上测量）。

Original abstract: Coding agents often pass per-prompt safety review yet ship exploitable code when their tasks are decomposed into routine engineering tickets. The challenge is structural: existing safety alignment evaluates overt requests in isolation, leaving models blind to malicious end-states that emerge from sequenced compliance with innocuous-looking requests. We introduce MOSAIC-Bench (Malicious Objectives Sequenced As Innocuous Compliance), a benchmark of 199 three-stage attack chains paired with deterministic exploit oracles on deployed software substrates (10 web-application substrates, 31 CWE classes, 5 programming languages) that treats both exploit ground truth and downstream reviewer protocol as first-class evaluation axes. On this benchmark, nine production coding agents from Anthropic, OpenAI, Google, Moonshot, Zhipu, and Minimax compose innocuous tickets at 53-86% end-to-end ASR with only two refusals across all staged runs. In a matched direct-prompt experiment over four frontier Claude/Codex agents, vulnerable-output rates fall to 0-20.4%: Claude primarily refuses, while Codex primarily hardens rather than emitting the vulnerable implementation - ticket staging silences both defense modes simultaneously. Downstream, code reviewer agents approve 25.8% of these confirmed-vulnerable cumulative diffs as routine PRs, and a full-context implementation protocol closes only 50% of the staged/direct gap, ruling out context fragmentation as the sole explanation. As a deployable but non-adaptive mitigation, reframing the reviewer as an adversarial pentester reduces evasion across the evaluated reviewer subset; pentester framed evasion ranges from 3.0% to 17.6%, and an open-weight Gemma-4-E4B-it reviewer under this framing detects 88.4% of attacks on the dataset with a 4.6% false-positive rate measured on 608 real-world GitHub PRs.

</details>


### [84] [Generating Proof-of-Vulnerability Tests to Help Enhance the Security of Complex Software](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03956v1)
*Shravya Kanchi,Xiaoyan Zang,Ying Zhang,Danfeng Yao,Na Meng*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: PoVSmith通过结合调用路径分析、示例测试和大语言模型，自动生成漏洞验证测试，有效发现并验证了Java应用中通过库漏洞可被利用的入口点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开发者需要具体可执行的PoV测试来判断库漏洞的实际风险，但手动构造困难，现有工具自动化不足。

Method: PoVSmith结合调用路径分析、示例测试、代码上下文和反馈，通过多个提示引导Codex和GPT进行测试生成、执行和评估，包含迭代代码精炼。

Result: 在33个Java程序对上，PoVSmith正确识别了96%的入口点和调用路径，生成的152个测试中有55%证明了可行的攻击方式，优于现有方法。

Conclusion: PoVSmith显著减少了人为参与并提高了测试质量，贡献了基于代理的测试生成、迭代精炼和LLM质量评估的新方法。

中文摘要：开发者在第三方库（Libs）之上创建现代软件应用程序（Apps）。当库漏洞通过应用程序代码可达时，应用程序可能易受软件供应链攻击。先前的研究表明，开发者通常需要具体且可执行的证据，即漏洞验证（PoV）测试，来判断报告的依赖漏洞是否对其应用程序构成实际安全风险。然而，手动构造此类测试具有挑战性，现有的工具支持不足以自动化该过程。为简化测试生成，我们创建了PoVSmith——一种新方法，它结合调用路径分析、示例测试、代码上下文和反馈，形成多个提示来引导编码代理（即Codex）和大语言模型（即GPT）进行测试生成、执行和评估。我们在33个⟨App, Lib⟩Java程序对上评估了PoVSmith，其中每个App依赖于一个有漏洞的Lib。PoVSmith发现了158个独特的应用程序级入口点（即公共方法）调用有漏洞的库API；其中152个（96%）被正确找到，同时调用路径也被正确识别。借助这些方法调用信息，PoVSmith生成了152个测试，其中84个（55%）展示了通过利用Lib漏洞攻击App的可行方式。PoVSmith显著优于最先进的基于LLM的方法，因为它减少了人为参与，同时大幅提高了测试质量。我们的工作贡献了：（1）一种基于代理的测试生成新方法，（2）由执行反馈驱动的迭代代码精炼过程，以及（3）基于测试上下文和执行日志的LLM质量评估。

Original abstract: Developers create modern software applications (Apps) on top of third-party libraries (Libs). When library vulnerabilities are reachable through application code, the applications can be vulnerable to software supply chain attacks. Prior work shows that developers often require concrete and executable evidence, i.e., proof-of-vulnerability (PoV) tests, to decide whether a reported dependency vulnerability poses a practical security risk to their application. However, manually crafting such tests is challenging, and existing tool support is insufficient to automate the procedure. To streamline test generation, we created PoVSmith -- a new approach that combines call path analysis, exemplar test, code context, and feedback into multiple prompts to guide a coding agent (i.e., Codex) and a large language model (i.e., GPT) for test generation, execution, and assessment. We evaluated PoVSmith on 33 $\langle$App, Lib$\rangle$ Java program pairs, where each App depends on a vulnerable Lib. PoVSmith revealed 158 unique application-level entry points (i.e., public methods) calling vulnerable library APIs; 152 (96\%) of them were correctly found, together with the call paths properly recognized. With such method call information, PoVSmith generated 152 tests, 84 (55\%) of which demonstrated feasible ways of attacking Apps by exploiting Lib vulnerabilities. PoVSmith substantially outperforms the state-of-the-art LLM-based approach, as it reduces human involvement while dramatically improving test quality. Our work contributes (1) a novel approach of agent-based test generation, (2) an iterative code refinement process driven by execution feedback, and (3) LLM-based quality assessment grounded in both the test context and execution logs.

</details>


### [85] [Identifier-Free Code Embedding Models for Scalable Search](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05251v1)
*Eric Wolos,Michael Doyle*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 通过对比学习微调Qwen3-Embedding模型，实现了源代码与反编译代码之间的双向函数关联，并在所有基线上取得大幅提升，同时泛化到未训练的常量算法关联任务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有搜索工具未充分利用AI能力，且先前嵌入模型工作未覆盖源代码与反编译代码的双向关联，需要填补这一空白。

Method: 形式化函数关联问题，使用对比学习微调Qwen3-Embedding模型来提升双向关联性能。

Result: 新模型在所有函数关联基线上显著优于其他模型，并泛化到未训练的常量算法关联任务。

Conclusion: 微调后的Qwen3-Embedding模型能有效实现源代码与反编译代码的双向关联，且具有良好的泛化能力。

中文摘要：函数关联是二进制逆向工程师的一个有用过程。存在搜索工具可以大规模执行关联，但它们没有充分利用AI搜索所提供的全部能力。先前的工作已经探索了为某些逆向工程代码表示之间的关联开发嵌入模型，但该工作并未涵盖源代码与经过标准预处理要求的剥离后的反编译代码之间的双向关联。为了弥补这一差距，我们形式化了这一函数关联问题，并评估了嵌入模型在这两种表示之间进行双向关联的程度。为了提升模型在此任务上的性能，我们使用对比学习微调了一个Qwen3-Embedding模型。我们发现，我们的新模型在所有函数关联基线上以显著优势优于其他模型，并且能够泛化到它未明确训练的常量算法关联任务上。

Original abstract: Function association is a useful process for binary reverse engineers. Search tools exist to perform association at scale, but they do not utilize the full range of capabilities that AI-enabled search provides. Prior work has explored the development of embedding models for association between certain reverse engineering code representations, but that work does not cover bidirectional association between source code and decompiled, stripped code with standard preprocessing requirements. To bridge this gap, we formalize this function association problem and evaluate the extent to which embedding models can bidirectionally associate between these two representations. To improve model performance at this task, we fine-tune a Qwen3-Embedding model with contrastive learning. We find that our new model outperforms other models on all function association baselines by a substantial margin and generalizes to a constant-algorithm association task it is not explicitly trained on.

### [86] [Root-Cause-Driven Automated Vulnerability Repair](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04251v1)
*Hulin Wang,Zion Leonahenahe Basque,Jie Hu,Ati Priya Bajaj,Yibo Liu,Samuel Zhu,Giorgi Kobakhia,Nikhil Chapre,Will Rosenberg,Siddharth Mishra,Aditya Maheshbhai Gabani,Moritz Schloegel,Adam Doupé,Yan Shoshitaishvili,Ruoyu Wang,Tiffany Bao*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: Kumushi通过结合动态故障定位与证据加权排序，在自动化漏洞修复中显著提升了根本原因修复的比例，并引入两级补丁质量评估以区分真正的修复与表面修复。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM修复代理易产生浅层编辑而非根本修复，且根本原因定位困难。

Method: 设计根因驱动的补丁代理Kumushi，使用多样化动态故障定位和证据加权排名聚焦LLM于缺陷相关代码；引入两级补丁质量度量（自动化Oracle验证+专家评估）。

Result: 在178个C/C++漏洞上，Kumushi在自动化评估中超越先前专用代理，匹配前沿商业代理；专家评估表明其产生更多根因修复，在大多数成对比较中胜出。

Conclusion: 自动化漏洞修复需要更强的修补系统和更丰富的评估方法以区分真正修复与表面修复。

中文摘要：近期基于LLM的系统使得自动化漏洞修复变得越来越实用，但仍存在两个挑战。首先，如果没有关于漏洞来源的强信号，修复代理会倾向于进行浅层编辑，以掩盖观察到的失效，而潜在缺陷仍然未解决。其次，找到漏洞的根本原因很困难：即使熟悉代码库的开发者也常常产生解决症状而非根本原因的修复，而基于LLM的代理在噪声更大的上下文和更少的程序理解下操作，也不例外。我们提出了Kumushi，一个根本原因驱动的补丁代理，通过结合多样化动态故障定位与证据加权排序，将LLM聚焦于与缺陷最相关的代码，以应对这两个挑战。为了严格衡量Kumushi是否产生真正更好的补丁，我们还引入了一个两级补丁质量度量指标，该指标将自动化Oracle验证与结构化的专家补丁评估配对。在178个C/C++漏洞上的评估中，Kumushi在自动化评估下显著优于先前的专门修复代理，并与前沿的商业编码代理相当。专家评估随后揭示了Oracle无法发现的差异：Kumushi产生更多根本原因修复和更少浅层补丁，并且在大多数决定性的成对比较中被优选。这些结果共同表明，自动化漏洞修复的进展不仅需要更强的补丁系统，还需要更丰富的评估方法，能够区分真正的修复与通过Oracle的修复。

Original abstract: Recent LLM-based systems have made automated vulnerability repair increasingly practical, but two challenges remain. First, without strong signals about where a bug originates, repair agents drift toward shallow edits that silence the observed failure while leaving the underlying defect unresolved. Second, finding the root cause for bugs is hard: even developers familiar with the codebase frequently produce fixes that address symptoms rather than the root cause, and LLM-based agents, operating with noisier context and less program understanding, are no exception. We present Kumushi, a root-cause-driven patching agent that addresses both challenges by combining diversified dynamic fault localization with evidence-weighted ranking to focus the LLM on the code most relevant to the defect. To rigorously measure whether Kumushi produces genuinely better patches, we also introduce a two-tier patch quality metric that pairs automated oracle validation with structured expert assessment of patches. Evaluated on 178 C/C++ vulnerabilities, Kumushi substantially outperforms prior specialized repair agents under automated evaluation while matching a frontier commercial coding agent. Expert assessment then reveals differences that oracles cannot: Kumushi produces more root-cause fixes and fewer superficial patches, and is preferred in the majority of decisive pairwise comparisons. Together, these results demonstrate that progress in automated vulnerability repair requires not only stronger patching systems, but also richer evaluation methods capable of distinguishing genuine fixes from oracle-passing ones.

</details>


### [87] [Lightweight Vulnerability Detection from Code Metrics and Token Features](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04260v1)
*Chun Yin Chiu*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 使用轻量级特征（token n-grams和代码度量）和逻辑回归进行函数级漏洞分类，在随机分割上表现尚可，跨项目泛化较差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多实际工作流程需要快速且可重现的排序基线以进行人工分类，而现有方法依赖重型表示。本研究旨在探索一个轻量级、透明且高效的基线方法。

Method: 结合稀疏token n-grams（TF-IDF）和六种简单代码度量（NLOC、近似圈复杂度、token计数、最大括号深度、参数计数），使用类别加权逻辑回归分类器，不使用深度学习或代码图。

Result: 随机分割PR-AUC 0.642，Recall@10% 0.161；跨项目（FFmpeg→QEMU）PR-AUC约0.436。消融实验显示特征贡献，标识符重命名影响，端到端效率高。

Conclusion: 简单特征可提供透明基线，但依赖于表面词汇，跨项目迁移有限。

中文摘要：C/C++代码的漏洞检测越来越依赖诸如代码图和深度模型等重型表示，而许多实际工作流程仍然受益于快速且可重现的排序基线以进行人工分类。本预印本研究了一个轻量级的函数级漏洞分类流程，该流程将原始函数文本中的稀疏token n-gram与一小部分廉价的代码度量相结合，包括NLOC、近似圈复杂度、token计数、最大括号深度和参数计数。我们使用TF-IDF token特征和类别加权逻辑回归分类器，避免了深度学习、Transformer和程序图。使用Devign函数级标签，我们评估了随机和跨项目设置，包括一个FFmpeg到QEMU的迁移实验。我们强调precision-recall AUC和Recall@10%作为针对倾斜或分类导向工作负载的排序指标。在随机分割中，最佳组合变体达到PR-AUC 0.642和Recall@10% 0.161，而跨项目泛化则更加困难，PR-AUC约为0.436。我们进一步报告了消融实验、仅测试的标识符重命名鲁棒性以及端到端效率。结果表明，简单的token和度量特征提供了一个有用的透明基线，但也暴露了对表面词汇线索的敏感性和有限的跨项目迁移能力。

Original abstract: Vulnerability detection for C/C++ code increasingly relies on heavy representations such as code graphs and deep models, while many practical workflows still benefit from fast and reproducible ranking baselines for human triage. This preprint studies a lightweight function-level vulnerability triage pipeline that combines sparse token n-grams from raw function text with a small set of inexpensive code metrics, including NLOC, approximate cyclomatic complexity, token count, maximum brace depth, and parameter count. We use TF-IDF token features and a class-weighted logistic regression classifier, avoiding deep learning, transformers, and program graphs.
  Using the Devign function-level labels, we evaluate random and cross-project settings, including a FFmpeg-to-QEMU transfer experiment. We emphasize precision-recall AUC and Recall@10% as ranking-oriented metrics for skewed or triage-oriented workloads. On the random split, the best combined variant reaches PR-AUC 0.642 and Recall@10% 0.161, while cross-project generalization is substantially harder, with PR-AUC around 0.436. We further report ablations, test-only identifier-renaming robustness, and end-to-end efficiency. The results suggest that simple token and metric features provide a useful transparent baseline, but also expose sensitivity to superficial lexical cues and limited cross-project transfer.

</details>
